***журчание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:журчание.html>журча́ние</a> (22509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчать.html>журча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žurčátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчание.html>журча́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žurčánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчание.html>журча́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчание.html>журча́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчание.html>журча́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>murmur, gurgling, babble (of water)</li></ol>

***журчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:журчать.html>журча́ть</a> (13047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журчать.html>журча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žurčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of water</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to babble, to purl, to murmur
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матрёнин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внезапно.html>внеза́пно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеплеть.html>потепле́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́зом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сталь.html>ста́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыры́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ны</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:журчать.html>журча́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ручей.html>ручьи́</a>, проры́вшиеся <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снегу́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоге́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голенище.html>голени́ще</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vnezápno poteplélo, v odín denʹ rázom raspustílo, stáli syrýje tumány, <b>žurčáli</b> ručʹí, prorývšijesja v snegú, i nogá v sapogé uvjazála po vsjó goleníšče</i></dd><dd>one day it suddently got warmer, fog disbanded and thinned, rivulets <b>purled</b>  parting the snow and whoever waded [through the snow] had his boots sunk whole</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***жуткий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткий</a> (3380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žútkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жу́тче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>horrifying, horrible, inducing a sense of horror
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сниться.html>сни́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сцена.html>сце́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчерашний.html>вчера́шнего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льма</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne vsju nočʹ snílisʹ éti <b>žútkije</b> scény iz včerášnevo fílʹma.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">All night, I was dreaming of the <b>horrifying</b> scenes from yesterday's movie.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horrible, bad, of poor quality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погода.html>пого́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>дворе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Žútkaja</b> pogóda na dvoré.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The weather is <b>horrible</b> outside.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> extreme
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорщик.html>спо́рщик</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>žútkij</b> spórščik.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is <b>extremely</b> argumentative.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́ткий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žútkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́тко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žútko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>frighteningly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> terribly, extremely</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́тко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žútko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one is terrified
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жуткий.html>жу́тко</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>žútko</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>am terrified</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>it is frightening

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жутко-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žutko-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жутковатый.html>жуткова́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žutkovátyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жуткова́тее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жуткова́тей</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> somewhat horrifying, somewhat creepy</li></ol>

***жуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жуть.html>жуть</a> (13839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">take, seize, grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġietan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">get</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χᾰνδᾰ́νω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khandánō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold, contain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hedera</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ivy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуть.html>жуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуть.html>жу́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуть.html>жу́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жуть.html>жу́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dismay, dread, horror</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жучок.html>жучо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žučók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жучок.html>жучка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жучок.html>жучки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жучок.html>жучко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жук.html>жук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span> (small) beetle, bug <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> home-made electrical fuse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bug, wiretap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an electronic intercept device</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="Технический жаргон">техн. жарг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезок.html>отре́зок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводника́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:восстанавливающий.html>восстана́вливающий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:контакт.html>конта́кт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электрический.html>электри́ческой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цепь.html>це́пи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обход.html>обхо́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сработавший.html>срабо́тавшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предохранитель.html>предохрани́теля</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***за.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> (23)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*za</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">za</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(of location) behind; beyond; on the other side of <span class="case-gov">(+ <i>instrumental</i>)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реко́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнышко.html>со́лнышко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́тся</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Za</b> rekój sólnyško sadítsja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sun is setting<i> </i><b>across</b> the river</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(of motion, <i>+ accusative case</i>) to</li>
<li>(of time, <i>+ accusative case</i>) during <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">close to <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:течение.html>тече́ние</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пребывание.html>пребыва́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> москве́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> vrémja prebyvánija v Moskvé</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>during</b> his stay in Moscow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> poslédnije dvádcatʹ let</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the past twenty years (lt. <b>during</b> the last twenty years)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(of time, + accusative case with <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a>) time before an event
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> dve minúty do uróka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">2 minutes (<b>left</b>) before the lecture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>+ accusative case</i>) for; to; by; after; over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On igrájet <b>za</b> komándu A.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's playing <b>for</b> team A.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бороться.html>боро́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">borótʹsja <b>za</b> mir</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fight <b>for</b> peace</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>+ accusative case</i>) instead of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекция.html>ле́кцию</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заболевший.html>заболе́вшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коллега.html>колле́гу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sevódnja on čitál lékciju <b>za</b> zabolévševo kollégu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Today he gave a lecture <b>for</b> a sick colleague.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(of voting, <i>+ accusative case</i>) in favor of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проголосовать.html>проголосова́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строительство.html>строи́тельство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лы</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On progolosovál <b>za</b> stroítelʹstvo nóvoj škóly.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He voted <b>for</b> the construction of a new school.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>+ instrumental case</i>) at; while
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> obédom razgovór šól o teátre</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>at</b> dinner the conversation turned to the theater</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужин.html>у́жином</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> úžinom</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>while</b> eating dinner</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игро́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> igrój</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>while</b> playing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> rabótoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>while</b> working</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> knígoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>while</b> reading (specifically a book)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтение.html>чте́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>za</b> čténijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>while</b> reading (nothing specific implied)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used in expressions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rádovatʹsja <b>za</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rejoice <b>for</b> someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бояться.html>боя́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bojátʹsja <b>za</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be afraid <b>for</b> someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> кого́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bratʹ kovó-libo <b>za</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take someone <b>by</b> the hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a> кого́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vestí kovó-libo <b>za</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead someone <b>by</b> the hand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***зааплодировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зааплодировать.html>зааплоди́ровать</a> (17117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодировать.html>аплоди́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aplodírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зааплодировать.html>зааплоди́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaaplodírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодировать.html>аплоди́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start clapping/applauding, to burst into applause</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забава.html>заба́ва</a> (6576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zabava</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забава.html>заба́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabáva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забава.html>заба́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забава.html>заба́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забава.html>заба́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fun, amusement, entertainment</li>
<li>pastime</li></ol>

***забарабанить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забарабанить.html>забараба́нить</a> (16477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барабанить.html>бараба́нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">barabánitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забегаловка.html>забега́ловка</a> (15119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегаловка.html>забега́ловка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabegálovka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегаловка.html>забега́ловки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегаловка.html>забега́ловки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегаловка.html>забега́ловок</a></b>)

***забегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забега́ть</a> (6118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to start running</li>
<li>to become shifty (of a look)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забежать.html>забежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative somewhere) by running or as if by running
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забега́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On káždyj denʹ <b>zabegájet</b> tudá péred rabótoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He runs that way every day before work.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run ahead (in anticipation), to run before someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne nádo <b>zabegátʹ</b> vperjód!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">No need to run ahead!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit, to drop in (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> on)</li></ol>

***забежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забежать.html>забежа́ть</a> (8473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забежать.html>забежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забегать.html>забега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative somewhere) by running or as if by running
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забежать.html>забежа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>zabežál</b> tudá péred rabótoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He ran that way before work.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run ahead (in anticipation), to run before someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забежать.html>забежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabežátʹ</b> vperjód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run ahead; to anticipate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit, to drop in (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> on)</li></ol>

***забеспокоиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забеспокоиться.html>забеспоко́иться</a> (10775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́иться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bespokóitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забеспокоиться.html>забеспоко́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabespokóitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to worry <i>(about)</i>, to begin to feel anxious/uneasy <i>(about)</i></li></ol>

***забивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забивать.html>забива́ть</a> (8627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забивать.html>забива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive in (nail), to hammer in, to nail up</li>
<li>to score (a goal)</li>
<li>to beat up</li>
<li>to slaughter</li>
<li>to block up, to stop up, to cram, to obstruct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to outdo, to surpass</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ignore; to give up on some (previous) intention</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reserve</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">страд.</span> к забить <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Чёрный шар должен забиваться в противоположную лузу. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="сленговое">сленг</span> (на что-либо) биться об заклад, спорить о чём-либо, делать ставку на что-либо <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Ну что, будем <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забиваться</span> на сегодняшний футбол? </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Если не <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забиваться</span> на конкретный софт, можно подобрать подходящий под твоё железо. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="сленговое">сленг</span> (на что-либо с кем-либо) уговариваться о чём-либо <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Давайте <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забиваться</span> на стрелку с ними послезавтра. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="сленговое">сленг</span> (о мышцах, конечностях) уставать, начинать болеть от нагрузки <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Без тренировки мышцы <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забиваются</span> на первой же горке. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшее</a>">устар.</span> оказываться где-либо, забираться куда-либо далеко поневоле, волею случая <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшее</a>">устар.</span> (умом во что-либо) пристально чем-либо заниматься, вникать во что-либо <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Он часто опускает важнейшие должности жизни, а <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забивается</span> умом в пустошные предметы. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>
<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="<a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a>">Синонимы</span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">частичн.</span>: забираться, прятаться</li>
<li>засоряться, закупориваться</li>
</ol>
